[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclarations. AddressSanitizer reports a [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m-byte read just past a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte heap [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation in the function `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The overflow [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs during parameter-entity expansion in `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue`, ultimately[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked by the fuzzer harness `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzz/xml.c`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue observed  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Running the libFuzzer target [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mxml[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m under AddressSanitizer with an XML seed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput causes a crash in `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`. The sanitizer log reports a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmulti-byte read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at address [0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[39m, which lies [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately beyond a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte region.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Heap-buffer-overflow during memory copy [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`__asan_memcpy`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the XML parser’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity handling code.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The faulty read size is [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes, but the buffer was allocated with only [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The small buffer originates from `xmlStrdup` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `xmlFuzzMalloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduplicating an entity value.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow arises in `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:777[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, called by [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:4005[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as part of entity value expansion.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The parser’s overall call chain includes:  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlParseEntityValue` → `xmlParseEntityDecl` → `xmlParseInternalSubset` → [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseDocument` → `xmlCtxtParseDocument`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Final invocation by `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/xml.[0m[1;92mc:68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Fuzzer configuration: interactive mode, libFuzzer engine, seed corpus disabled,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m, custom dictionary [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xml.dict`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Impacted code areas for investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` in parser.c — buffer sizing, boundary checks, and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemcpy usage.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Parameter-entity expansion logic in `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` and [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseEntityValue` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Entity declaration parsing in `xmlParseEntityDecl` and [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlParseInternalSubset`.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Memory allocation and string duplication functions: `xmlFuzzMalloc` [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/fuzz.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `xmlStrndup`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`xmlStrdup` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlstring.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Entity creation and storage in `xmlCreateEntity`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`xmlAddEntity` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentities.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness integration at `fuzz/xml.[0m[1;92mc:68[0m[39m` to understand how inputs reach [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe parser.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue indicates a mismatch between allocated buffer size and the amount of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata copied during entity expansion. A thorough review of buffer management in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity-handling routines is recommended to understand the full scope of the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
